    def test_priority_chain(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
    ) -> None:
        """Source priority order."""
        value_file = write_text(tmp_path / "port.txt", "  42  \n")
        schema_path = _write_schema(
            tmp_path,
            {
                "host": {
                    "type": "string",
                    "default": "localhost",
                    "env": "CFGPIPE_CP1_HOST",
                    "arg": "host",
                },
                "port": {
                    "type": "integer",
                    "default": "3000",
                    "env": "CFGPIPE_CP1_PORT",
                    "file": str(value_file),
                    "arg": "port",
                },
            },
        )
    
        result = run_cfgpipe(
            entrypoint_argv,
            schema_path=schema_path,

                "CFGPIPE_CP1_PORT": "5000",
            },
            arg_candidates=["--host=arg-host", "-port=7000"],
            cwd=tmp_path,
        )
    
>       assert_success(result)

        unreadable_path.mkdir()

            tmp_path,
            {
                "port": {

                    "default": "3000",

                }
            },
        )

entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', '--project', '/workspace', '/workspace/cfgpipe.py']
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_primary_store_resolves_de0')
store_server = RunningStoreServer(address='http://127.0.0.1:46225', _harness=<conftest.StoreHarness object at 0x71228d6da6c0>)
store_key = 'cfg/name', param_key = 'name', param_type = 'string'
value = 'store-name', version = 2, default = 'fallback'

    @pytest.mark.functionality
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        ("store_key", "param_key", "param_type", "value", "version", "default"),
        [
            ("cfg/name", "name", "string", "store-name", 2, "fallback"),
            ("config/port-number", "api_port", "integer", "8088", 3, None),
            ("cfg/name", "name", "string", "", 1, "fallback"),
            ("cfg/port", "port", "integer", "9001", 0, None),
            ("cfg/feature flag&name", "feature_name", "string", "enabled", 2, None),
        ],
        ids=[
            "default-fallback",
            "key-mismatch",
            "empty-string",
            "version-zero",
            "url-encoded",
        ],
    )
    def test_primary_store_resolves(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
        store_server,
        store_key: str,
        param_key: str,
        param_type: str,
        value: str,
        version: int,
        default: str | None,
    ) -> None:
        """Primary-store lookup across variants."""
        store_server.set_primary(store_key, value, version=version)
        field: dict[str, object] = {"type": param_type, "primary-store": store_key}
        if default is not None:
            field["default"] = default
        schema_path = _write_schema(tmp_path, {param_key: field})
    
        result = run_cfgpipe(
            entrypoint_argv,
            schema_path=schema_path,
            global_args=["--primary-store", store_server.address],
            cwd=tmp_path,
        )
    
>       assert_success(result)

            ("config/port-number", "api_port", "integer", "8088", 3, None),

            ("cfg/port", "port", "integer", "9001", 0, None),
            ("cfg/feature flag&name", "feature_name", "string", "enabled", 2, None),
        ],
        ids=[
            "default-fallback",
            "key-mismatch",
            "empty-string",
            "version-zero",
            "url-encoded",
        ],
    )
    def test_primary_store_resolves(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
        store_server,
        store_key: str,
        param_key: str,
        param_type: str,
        value: str,
        version: int,
        default: str | None,
    ) -> None:
        """Primary-store lookup across variants."""
        store_server.set_primary(store_key, value, version=version)
        field: dict[str, object] = {"type": param_type, "primary-store": store_key}
        if default is not None:
            field["default"] = default
        schema_path = _write_schema(tmp_path, {param_key: field})
    
        result = run_cfgpipe(
            entrypoint_argv,
            schema_path=schema_path,
            global_args=["--primary-store", store_server.address],
            cwd=tmp_path,
        )

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x71228cb25010>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty

.evaluation_tests/utils.py:216:

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x71228cd8bb60>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x71228cd884d0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).

                    raise Empty

                    self.not_empty.wait()

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x71228caa8aa0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x71228ca7f560>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty
